Local News Two

A Bathhouse Customer Commits Suicide by Poison 127

First Deceived by a Friend

Then Deceived by a Military Officer

Two Suicide Attempts, But Both Times Survives

A Strange and Laughable Suicide Note

Yesterday afternoon around 7 PM, a bathhouse named He Qingchi, located at number 58 Datong Road, Zhabei, was visited by a customer who appeared to be around twenty years old and was wearing very thin clothing. After bathing, he lay down on a couch and remained there for a long time without moving. A staff member, suspecting something was wrong, approached him and noticed a strange color in his face, fearing that he had taken poison. He immediately reported this to the bathhouse owner, Feng Guozhen, who then summoned police officers from post number seven. The officers transported the bathhouse customer to Pushan Hospital, where doctors determined that he had ingested opium. They immediately administered emergency treatment, reviving him and enabling him to speak. He was then transferred to the Fourth District Public Security Bureau for questioning. According to his own account, his surname was Li, his given name was Jinming, and he was 24 years old. He was originally from Anhui and currently resided at number 2, Shipai Lane, outside of Changmen, Suzhou. He had previously served as the director of the Wujiang Detention Center but was dismissed after a disagreement with his superiors. He returned to his hometown, and last month managed to scrape together several dozen yuan for travel expenses, packed a bag of belongings, and came to Shanghai to seek employment. A friend named Wang Xingming, whom he had met in Suzhou, accompanied him and resided with him at a certain hotel near the North Station. However, Wang suddenly had malicious intentions and lured him to an amusement park for entertainment, while at the same time secretly stealing his luggage and silver dollars without a trace. At this point, he had lost both his possessions and his wealth and felt extremely discouraged. However, he still did not want to return to his hometown immediately, to avoid being laughed at. Therefore, the next day he went to a certain school in Brahma Ferry to visit a friend, making a final appeal. Because the address was unclear, he was unable to find the school and returned disappointed. Alone, he walked forward, encountering a small river. He then resolved to commit suicide by jumping into the river, seeking death. However, death did not come, and instead, he encountered a philanthropist named Mr. Wang, who gave him five yuan and urged him to return home and not take his life lightly. He returned to the North Station, abandoning the path to death and instead seeking to join the military. He encountered someone dressed as a military officer, who told him that if he wanted to join the army, he must first get equipped. The five yuan in his pocket was then handed over to the military officer, who led him to the entrance of the Sincere Company on Nanjing Road and told him to wait a moment. The military officer then went inside to purchase military supplies but never returned. At this point, he knew he had been deceived again. With no way forward or backward, he had no choice but to pawn his close-fitting undershirt and pants for six dimes, finding temporary lodging at a small hotel for one night. With the remaining money, he purchased opium and went to the bathhouse to commit suicide, he said. A suicide note was found in Li's pocket, along with slips of paper containing anti-Japanese slogans and national salvation strategies. The handwriting in the suicide note was extremely潦草(liaocao - sloppy/cursive), and the writing was incoherent. The main idea was divided into three sections. The first section described how he had been lured and deceived by a treacherous friend, leading him to seek death. The second section stated that his family should not send anyone to Shanghai to handle his affairs after his death. The final section called out to his beloved mother, repeatedly, and stated that after his death, he would forever protect his mother's health. The letter ended there, but the signature at the end was surprisingly unexpected. After the three characters for "short-lived male," the English signature style, a transliteration of "Li Jinming," was appended. The date at the end of the letter, "12.12.4" in Arabic numerals, complemented the English signature, creating a unique style in a suicide note. The other two papers contained anti-Japanese slogans and popular writings of a national salvation nature, which were unremarkable compared to his vivid description of his suicide attempt.

Family Suffers from Coal Poisoning 128

Li Wu Dies From Excessive Poisoning

Li Guitang, 37 years old, from Shaoxing, and his wife, Wu, 27 years old, along with their son Jinxiang, 7 years old, and a newborn daughter just over two months old, totaling five family members, lived at 48 Xinzha Road near the Gordon Road intersection in Shanghai. Last night, after dinner, because the weather was severely cold, they moved the coal briquette stove into the room to keep warm. Shortly afterward, the doors were closed tightly, and the whole family went to sleep peacefully. However, the coal gas permeated the small room, and after prolonged exposure, they all suffered from coal poisoning and lost consciousness. Around 10 PM, a friend surnamed Ma arrived and knocked on the door several times but received no response. However, he saw coal gas flowing out from the cracks in the door. Initially suspecting a fire, he managed to pry open the door and entered the room, finding the entire family unconscious. Knowing that it was likely coal poisoning, he summoned neighbors to hire a car and transport them to Baolong Hospital for treatment. After examination, the others were found to be unharmed, but Wu, due to excessive poisoning, could not be saved and died half an hour later.

Preparation for the County National Goods Exhibition 129

The Shanghai County People's Education Center sent a letter yesterday to the National Goods Factory Federation, stating that the brutal Japanese invasion is deeply hated by the people. In addition to armed resistance, economic severance is also a sound strategy for saving the country. At a time when the call to use domestic goods is reaching the heavens, our domestic goods industry should strive to manufacture goods to meet the demand. However, the public's ability to distinguish between domestic goods and foreign goods is weak, and unscrupulous merchants may inevitably mix the bad with the good. To enhance the public's knowledge and increase their patriotism, the center has decided to hold the first Shanghai County National Goods Exhibition for one week, starting on New Year's Day of the 21st year. After the exhibition closes, the exhibits will be preserved to create a display room for regular rotating exhibitions to promote the use of domestic goods. Our resources are limited, and collection is difficult. We request your federation's strong assistance to ensure its success.

Tobacco and Exchange Industry Continues to Request Exemption from Business Tax 130

The Municipal Tobacco and Exchange Industry Association has submitted another petition to the Municipal Government, stating that they respectfully follow the Ministry's approval, and, in accordance with the regulations of your government, the tobacco and exchange industry should be exempted from business tax. They are again submitting a request for review and approval, and to be ordered to comply. The association received a document from the Ministry of Finance, number 14174, stating that a petition had been submitted requesting that the tobacco and exchange industry be exempted from business tax. The Municipal Finance Bureau rejected this petition, and a special request was made for interpretation and exemption. After an investigation, it was found that after the promulgation of the business tax law, the central government collected tobacco and alcohol sales taxes, reserving one-tenth for the central government and allocating the rest to the provinces and cities as local revenue. The measures for the exemption of business taxes on the tobacco and alcohol industries have been newly revised. All shops that primarily engage in the sale of cigarettes or alcohol and also sell other goods, where the main business has already paid tobacco and alcohol license taxes, should have their business tax excluded and exempted. As for other part-time businesses, business tax should be levied in accordance with the established case. It was requested that the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau be ordered to comply, and that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce be notified. In response to this document, the association investigated the businesses of its members, finding that tobacco is the main part of their business, with other part-time goods accounting for approximately 20-30% on average. The annual business income is less than ten yuan. Now that the Ministry has approved a new revision, excluding and exempting the main part, it is consistent with the regulations of Article 3, paragraph 2 of your government's published tax ordinance (any business with an annual business income of less than one thousand yuan is exempted from business tax), and Article 8 (the business should be based on its main part to determine the business), the main part of the tobacco and exchange industry is tobacco, which has already been excluded and exempted, so the exemption of business tax for other part-time goods is undoubtedly based on the aforementioned two articles. Moreover, Shanghai is a special area, and its situation is different from the interior, so it cannot be compared. In recent years, commerce has declined, and making a living has become difficult. If more burdens are added, how can they maintain their livelihoods? It is hoped that your government will consider the difficulties of businesses and not reject the repeated requests of the association. The association, representing all members and businesses, humbly submits another request for review and approval. It is hoped that your government will order the Finance Bureau to exempt the tobacco and exchange industry from business tax, and all business owners will be extremely grateful and await your orders. This is a urgent appeal, awaiting your instructions.

Wang Yansong's Resignation Speech 131

Wang Yansong, a supervisory committee member of the Municipal Party Headquarters, recently submitted his resignation as a committee member of the Municipal Party Headquarters. He made a statement to the press, saying that he had been promoting party principles in his spare time from business, but he was ashamed of his lack of knowledge and unable to help with the current difficulties. He had repeatedly requested to resign from his position in the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, but due to the supervision of the Central Committee, the retention of comrades, and the urging of business colleagues to express the pain of industry and commerce and to plan for labor-management coordination, he had reluctantly done his best. However, the trend of the times is increasingly chaotic, and his talent is insufficient for the heavy responsibility, making him fear failure. Fortunately, the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters executive and supervisory committee members have already submitted a request for collective resignation to the Central Committee. He, Wang Yansong, is happy to fulfill his initial wish, take a short rest, and devote himself to industrial and commercial endeavors and the development of the national economy, hoping to make a small contribution to strengthening national power. He deeply hopes that all comrades in the city and colleagues in the business community will acknowledge his sincerity, provide supervision, and be infinitely grateful.

Zhang Huabang Customs Radio Station Reports Weather Conditions 132

Sends Telegram to Jinan Meteorological Observatory

The Zhang Huabang Customs River Affairs Office of the Shanghai Customs recently received an order from the Customs Commissioner to report the local daily weather conditions, such as wind, rain, and sunshine, via radio to the Jinan Meteorological Observatory in Shandong Province at 6 AM and 2 PM every day, starting from the middle of this month, to provide a reference for the climate in the north and south and to assist in identification. It is said that this is also very important for airplanes. Therefore, in recent days, the staff of the River Affairs Office have been meticulously recording the weather, including the clarity of the sky, the presence and direction of wind, including sudden gusts, the direction of the wind (east, west, south, or north), and the amount and timing of rainfall, in a detailed register. The staff report twice daily.

Fires in Western and Northern Shanghai Last Night 133

Inside and Outside Cotton Mills: The Inside and Outside Cotton Mills Number One and Number Two on Robison Road in Western Shanghai have thousands of workers. Yesterday was Sunday, and no one was at the factory. Unexpectedly, at 8 PM, the four-story building suddenly caught fire. The chief of the Sixth District Police Station, seeing the situation, immediately ran to inform Inspector Gu, who reported to the Sixth District Headquarters. Chief Ren personally arrived with the police brigade and patrol team to investigate. However, the fire had already spread and was out of control. Fire trucks from Putuo Road, Jing'an Temple, and the Old Gate, along with Chinese and Western detectives from the Public Security Bureau, worked hard to extinguish the fire, which burned for two hours, causing traffic on Route 16 trolleybuses to be interrupted. Eleven foreign-style houses were burned down, and it is said that the losses were very heavy.

Robison Road: Furthermore, the newly built Shikumen houses behind the branch of the Grand Self-Sounding Clock Salt Industry Bank on Robison Road in Western Shanghai, which had not yet been completed, unexpectedly caught fire last night at 10 PM, spreading to the residences of neighbors surnamed Wang and Wu. Everyone was already asleep at the time, and when they awoke, it was too late to escape, so they had to jump out of the windows. As a result, a man surnamed Wu was seriously injured. The police transported him to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. Three houses were destroyed in the fire.

East of the Sun Temple: The straw shed without a number east of the Sun Temple in Zhabei, where tenant Liu Dacha lived, suddenly caught fire last night at 11 PM for unknown reasons. The weather was cold and windy, and there was no running water nearby, making it difficult for the fire trucks to extinguish the fire. As a result, the fire was very fierce, spreading to more than fifty straw sheds. The fire was finally extinguished at 1 AM this morning. The suspected arsonist, Liu Dacha, has been arrested by the police and is being interrogated.

Pig Butchers Arrive in Pudong 134

Out-of-Town Tenants with Bad Intentions

At 7 PM the day before yesterday, five or six out-of-town tenants suddenly jumped ashore from a rowing boat at the Lujiazui Wharf in Pudong. Detective Zhang Yong, Yang Jinsheng, and Chen Jiafu of the Third District Public Security Bureau, acting on instructions, were inspecting pedestrians at the wharf. A six-round handgun with three bullets was found on Li Miaosheng. Three Frozen to Death Due to Cold Weather 135

(1) The weather has suddenly become very cold in recent days. Around 9 PM the night before last, an unidentified elderly man, about 50 years old, collapsed near the intersection of Route Massenet and Route Tenant de Tour in the French Concession (east of the Second Special District Prison) due to the cold and inability to walk. Collision Incident Involving Ship Due to Rising Tide and Strong Wind 136

Zhengzhou Ship Crashes Into Wharf Ship

A Ship Sinks to the Bottom with Cargo

Around 2:30 PM the day before yesterday, the Chinese merchant ship Zhengzhou, arriving in Shanghai from abroad, sailed to the outside of the Yitaixing warehouse wharf in Lijiadu, Pudong. At that time, it was a rising tide, and the north wind was unusually strong. The water was aided by the wind, and its force was even greater. The Zhengzhou ship sailed with the tide, causing the rudder to fail. The ship could not control itself and crashed into the Yitaixing wharf. Six or seven coal wharf ships were parked outside the wharf, and they were damaged in succession by the Zhengzhou ship. The damaged parts varied. Among them, two wharf ships hired by the Tianzhang Paper Mill, each carrying 50 tons of coal, suffered severe damage. Water immediately flooded the ships, and the entire ships and cargo sank to the bottom. Other ships belonging to Pu'an Public Security and Wanglinji, some loaded with coal and some empty, suffered varying degrees of damage. Yesterday, the affected parties requested the water police to investigate.

Collection Agent Embezzles Over Twelve Thousand Gold 141

Sentenced to Six Months Imprisonment

Wu Qinghe, from Changzhou, was a collection agent for the Tianzhang Paper Mill at 6 Sichuan Road. Recently, the manager of the mill, Luo Changkai, discovered that Wu had privately collected over two thousand yuan in payments, so he reported it to the General Police Station, ordering Detective Feikelun to arrest Wu and escort him to the First Special Court for investigation and detention. Yesterday morning, Judge Xu Jiashi continued the hearing in the criminal court. The lawyer for the police station, Ru Baoyi, stated that the plaintiff in this case initially only discovered that the defendant had embezzled over two thousand yuan. However, after the plaintiff carefully reviewed the accounts, it was discovered that Wu Qinghe had actually embezzled over twelve thousand yuan, for which detailed accounts were available. He requested that the court review the accounts and submitted them as evidence. Luo Changkai then submitted a report and questioned Wu Qinghe, who admitted that he had privately used all the amounts listed on the accounts presented by the plaintiff. Judge Xu reviewed the evidence and announced the judgment in court: Wu Qinghe was sentenced to six months' imprisonment for embezzling assets under his management in the course of his duties. The number of days spent in custody before the judgment is confirmed will be deducted from the sentence at a rate of two days for every one day of imprisonment.

Yesterday afternoon at 1:57 PM, a tram owned by Huashang Sanyuan Road, was approaching the Ximen station to stop, when two sisters and a six-year-old boy were walking past. Robbery with Injury Within the Second District 143

A Desperate Thief Fires Three Shots and Flees

Feng Shihua, 28 years old, from Beiping, is currently working as a messenger at Xie's residence at No. 87 Wanyi Fang, Luban Road, French Concession. Around 9 PM last night, Feng went to Lujiawan to visit a friend alone. When he arrived at Xu Jia Hui Road Bangingkou, just as he entered the Chinese district, three robbers suddenly jumped out of the dark alley, showing guns and forbidding any noise. They dragged Feng into the alley, first robbing him of the ten yuan bill stored in his pocket, and then attempted to take off his clothes. At this point, Feng became anxious and desperately resisted. The robbers then fired three shots at him. Feng was shot in the buttocks and immediately collapsed in pain. Police officers at the nearby police post heard the alert and rushed to the scene, but the robbers had already fled in the meantime. The police immediately transported Feng to the Liyuan Road Police Station of the Second District Headquarters and then transferred him to Baolong Hospital. It is reported that the bullet is still lodged in his abdomen, and his condition is very critical.

Tax Police in Zhabei Commemorate Battalion Commander Xie 144

Xie Mingdan, the battalion commander of the Second Battalion of the First Regiment of the Tax Police stationed in Zhabei, previously, while on horseback near the Wusong railway tracks, attempted to save a woman. The horse's tail touched a small train, causing a tragic accident where he was run over and killed. Yesterday at 9:35 AM, the regiment held a memorial service at the Maigen Road drill ground. Those in attendance included Chief Commander Wang, Chief of Staff Wang, Regiment Commanders Zhao and Gu of the First and Second Regiments, the Tsinghua Alumni Association, and dozens of other organizations, as well as Battalion Commander Xie's family, Xie Minghui, German advisor Shao Ke Pan (transliteration), dozens of other guests, and approximately 3,000 soldiers, battalion commanders, and company commanders from the First Regiment. The memorial ceremony proceeded as follows: (1) Military review; (2) Opening of the meeting; (3) All stand in silence; (4) Music played and firecrackers set off; (5) Officiant takes position; (6) Bow to the portrait; (7) Flower presentation; (8) Reading of the eulogy; (9) Ceremony concludes with music; (10) Speeches, details omitted; (11) Photograph; (12) Adjournment. Many condolences, wreaths, and other sacrificial items were sent by various sectors. Battalion Commander Xie's family is in dire straits, and assistance is greatly needed for the education of his orphans. Therefore, some people are initiating a fundraising campaign for the late Battalion Commander Xie to support the widow and orphans.

Perjury in a Murder Case 145

Zhang Qingxiang, the son of the late Zhang Linsen of Huayuanshi Bridge, Pudong, conspired with his maternal uncle, Zhang Quansheng, to seize the inheritance. They shot and injured his elder brother, Zhang Guoxiang, and killed his second brother, Zhang Yuxiang. The local court detained the defendants. Unexpectedly, Zhang Quansheng presented a false alibi, claiming that when Zhang Yuxiang was killed, he was at home drinking with Lu Liansheng, Yan Zilin, and Yan Xinglin. After Prosecutor Shen summoned and questioned them separately, their descriptions of the liquor differed. Some said it was sorghum wine, others said Wu Jiapi liquor, others said Shaoxing wine, and others said green bean liquor, creating a contradictory picture of red, green, yellow, and white. Regarding the side dishes, some said it was pork knuckle, others said chunks of meat, others said meatballs, and others said shredded meat, with inconsistencies in size. The interrogating officer determined that the evidence was false, and Zhang Quansheng was remanded in custody and denied visitors to prevent collusion.

French Police Apprehend Large Group of Bandits 146

Yesterday at 2 PM, Inspector General Jin Jiulin, Detective Li Yaolong, Deputy Detectives Mao Jingen, Zhang Ziying, Qian Yumin, and patrol detectives Cai Jinzhang and Qin Youyu of the French Police Special Unit, received a confidential tip from an informant that Anhui bandits Yang Guochun and Xiao Sanzi had committed numerous crimes in the city. They learned that the two bandits would pass through the Cishi Street area that afternoon and requested immediate dispatch of officers. Upon receiving the report, the detectives immediately rushed to the scene and waited. Around 4 PM, the two bandits appeared and were arrested. A six-inch Browning pistol and a revolver, along with over ten bullets, were found on their persons. They were taken to the police station and interrogated. They confessed that their accomplice, Chen Liwu, from the same village, was hiding at No. 46 Ma Xing Lane in the city. The detectives requested assistance from the Public Security Bureau and successfully arrested Chen at the address. A Mauser pistol with live ammunition was found. Chen confessed to over ten robberies, including the Zhongnan Socks Factory on Avenue Edward VII. Subsequently, over ten more accomplices and suspected criminals were arrested and temporarily detained at the police station, awaiting transfer to the court for interrogation.

Over four hundred party members and guests attended. Guests Ye Zhaojun, Xia Renqi, and Yuan Shizhao all gave poignant speeches. Zhu Ping'an, the district instructor, tearfully encouraged comrades with Ge's revolutionary spirit.

Young Woman Angrily Leaves Husband 149

Forced into Prostitution by Fellow Villager

Wang, the wife of Xie Xianlin from Ningbo, is a beautiful young woman. On the 11th of last month, the Xie couple had a quarrel over a trivial matter. In a fit of anger, Wang left her husband and intended to take a train to Shanghai. Upon arriving at the station, she met Zhang Xianghua, a woman from the same village. Zhang asked Wang why she wanted to go to Shanghai, and Wang explained the situation. Zhang offered to accompany her to Shanghai and help her find work. Wang believed her and went to Shanghai with her, residing at a certain address in Qinghefang, Hubei Road. Zhang had several fashionable dresses made for Wang and then forced her into prostitution. Wang, unfamiliar with the area and unable to seek help, deeply regretted leaving her husband and being deceived by a wicked person. However, it was too late. Reluctantly, she agreed to Zhang's request and went to various hotels every night to engage in prostitution. All the money she earned was given to Zhang. After his wife disappeared, Xie Xianlin asked his Shanghai friends, Wang Zhixiao and Dai Renzhi, to help him find her. After being entrusted, Wang and Dai searched diligently and recently discovered Wang's whereabouts. They sent a letter to Xie. After receiving the letter, Xie traveled to Shanghai and stayed with Wang and Dai in Room 613 of the Central Hotel on Hubei Road. He ordered the tea boy to summon Zhang Xianghua and Wang. Zhang, thinking it was business, happily brought Wang to Central Room 613. Xie, seeing that the prostitute was indeed his wife, became furious and detained Zhang. He reported the matter to the Laozha Police Station and ordered detectives to arrest Zhang and bring her to the police station. Yesterday, she was sent to the summary court of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer Qian Xunjiu explained the case and requested severe punishment according to Articles 146 and 248 of the Criminal Code. Xie and Wang testified. When questioned, Zhang confessed without hesitation. Judge Cheng Shangfeng verified the confession and sentenced Zhang Xianghua to five months in prison as a warning. Xie and Wang were released to Xie Xianlin.

Young Woman Attempts Suicide After Argument with Husband 150

Shen Gu, a young woman from Suzhou, 18 years old, worked as a nanny at No. 12 Taipingfang, Avenue Joffre, French Concession. Yesterday, she had an argument with her husband. Afterwards, she attempted suicide by swallowing opium. At 4 PM, a fellow villager arrived and took her to Jishi Hospital for treatment, but it was too late. She died around 10 PM that evening. The hospital reported the incident to the Zizhong Police Station, which ordered officers to transfer the body to the morgue for examination.

Shangbao Collects Vehicle Stamp Tax 151

The Jiangsu Shangbao Stamp Tax Bureau issued a notice stating: It is hereby notified that the vehicle license plates should be subject to stamp tax, which is stipulated in the regulations and should have been followed accordingly. Due to the vast area of Shangbao and the large number of vehicles, inspection has been difficult, resulting in inconsistent compliance with this national tax. This bureau has agreed with the Shanghai Public Utilities Bureau to assist in collecting the stamp tax when issuing vehicle licenses for the 21st year. The stamp tax will be stamped on the licenses as proof for easy inspection. The agreed-upon method has been submitted to the Jiangsu Stamp and Tobacco Tax Bureau and approved by the Ministry of Finance. The various vehicle licenses will be issued by the Public Utilities Bureau on specific dates, and the stamp tax will be collected at the same time. To ensure that license holders are aware, this notice is issued in advance. The vehicle licenses subject to stamp tax and the corresponding tax rates are listed below. All vehicle owners and operators must be aware of this and bring the tax amount to the Public Utilities Bureau when applying for the 21st year vehicle license, pay the tax in full, and have the license stamped for easy travel and identification. This bureau will dispatch personnel to inspect at any time. If any vehicle license subject to stamp tax is found without the tax paid and the stamp affixed, it will be confiscated and punished according to regulations, without leniency. Please comply with this notice. The vehicle licenses subject to stamp tax and the corresponding tax rates are as follows: 1. Automobile license: Stamp tax of 2 yuan. All automobiles for passenger or cargo transport, whether rented or privately owned, must be registered. 2. Carriage license: Stamp tax of 1 yuan. 3. Private rickshaw license: Stamp tax of 30 cents. 4. Bicycle license: Stamp tax of 20 cents. 5. Motorized bicycle license: Stamp tax of 20 cents. Temporarily subject to the bicycle tax rate. The stamp tax for the above vehicle licenses must be paid in full when applying for the license.

Hengyisheng, located at the intersection of Tiantong Road and Wusong Road in Hongkou, is promoting domestic goods by offering genuine discounts on domestic silk thread and various domestic cold-weather wool products, such as wool sweaters, wool socks, scarves, gloves, and thermal underwear, starting from December 1st for one month. Publication of "Wu Mai's Collected Works" 153

Lawyer Wu Mai has been tirelessly advocating for the recovery of legal rights for the past year. Wherever he went, the people's spirits were greatly roused. Mr. Wu is currently the director of the Propaganda Department of the City Anti-Japanese Association and has given impassioned speeches at various large and small schools and organizations in and outside the city. His spirit is so moving that listeners are inspired to action. Mr. Wu recently told people, "The country is in such a state, what glory is there in living and what sorrow is there in dying for us citizens? Everyone is willing to die, everyone should die, and everyone is determined to save the country without considering personal gain or loss. What is there we dare not do, what is there we dare not say? Let everyone move forward with a fearless spirit." His words were often filled with indignation. His letters, articles, poems, lyrics, and couplets related to the nation, the people, and the public good have been compiled by his friend Liu Yuanlin and published under the title "Wu Mai's Collected Works" last month. His diaries from previous years are being organized by his friend Xu Wancheng, secretary of the National Advancement Society, and will be published in a few days, destined to be enjoyed by young people. This is not Wu Mai boasting of his literary talent, but rather a desire to inspire the people. "Wu Mai's Collected Works" are available for sale at various bookstores, including Dadong and Qingyun, at a price of 25 cents. Mail orders or bulk purchases can be sent directly to Xu Wancheng, Shanghai Women's Middle School, West Gate, and will be sent immediately.

Li Li Initiates War Savings 158

The well-known socialite in Tianjin and Beijing, Ms. Li Li, felt that national affairs were deteriorating every day and was nervous. Mr. Zhang Shuiqi's Letter 160

(The Relationship Between the Japanese Cabinet Reorganization and Our Country)

The chief culprit of killing the Korean Empress Min, Adachi Kenzo, and his decades-old comrades have disagreed and brought down the Minseito cabinet, and organized a joint cabinet of various parties. He was originally a member of the Kokken party, and his views are different from those of Wakatsuki, who is backed by financial capitalists. With the success of this campaign, his foreign policy will inevitably be tougher, using the excuse of national unity to carry out the long-cherished aspirations of the Japanese people for decades. The Japanese people's aggressive stance is becoming increasingly prepared, but what about our country? The dawn of the Kuomintang's unification has just appeared, and the dark clouds have re-emerged. The rift between the government and the people is not only not disappearing, but is deepening day by day. Officials are lax and debauched, and they have not slightly changed the tyranny against the people, but instead are more arbitrary and self-serving. Patriotic students are arbitrarily beaten and robbed, and the people's mouthpiece is arbitrarily destroyed. The glorious proclamations declare the rule of law, but the party officials are the first to break the law. It is the people who want national unity, but the government does not allow it. The enemy is plotting against us, so urgently, what is the mentality of the ruling party that they have such actions?

(Note) The new Japanese cabinet has been ordered by Inukai Tsuyoshi to organize a joint cabinet. Some people are opposing it. All this has been seen in yesterday's newspaper. Mr. Zhang's letter has a very accurate and profound point of view. Therefore, it is shared with general readers.

Mr. Ding Qiuzhen's Letter (Opposing the Economic Commission's Cooperation with the League of Nations) 161

The recent cooperation between the Economic Commission, which has recently been established in our country, and the League of Nations is tantamount to providing the stronger with weapons of economic aggression and the international joint management of the book policy. The evils are very profound, and the troubles are endless. The Economic Commission covers all industrial construction in our country, with a very wide scope. Now, if we cooperate with the League of Nations, we will directly entrust foreign experts to handle all matters needed for our country's material survival, as well as important policies such as education and health, just like the previous examples of the customs, post office, and salt administration. Therefore, the loss of national sovereignty is no less than Japan's invasion of our Northeast. However, few Chinese people pay attention to it. It is truly strange. I deeply hope that my compatriots will think about saving it, so as to avoid danger.

Weather Report 164

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The Shandong coast is cloudy and cold, the Yangtze River basin and south of Ma'anshan are sunny and very cold, with localized fog. There are strong seasonal winds from the northwest to northeast in the Yellow Sea and East China Sea. The northeast wind in the Taiwan Strait is extremely strong. In addition, within 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 35.6 and the lowest was 20.0. Last year, the highest temperature on the same day was 49.1 and the lowest was 35.4.

Social News

The Paradise-like Leprosarium at Penang Island 165

My friend Zhang Saojun, residing in Penang Island overseas, recently reported to me about the leprosarium there. He said that patients receiving treatment in the hospital not only have no worries about food, clothing, and shelter, but they can also participate in recreational teams, music organizations, and enjoy the convenience of planting, animal husbandry, and smoking. It is no less than a paradise outside the world. I believe that the organization of the hospital is very beneficial to those who are unfortunate and disabled by illness among us humans, so I will introduce it here.

Mount Erskine on Penang Island is the most common residence for pitiful leprosy patients. In addition to having no worries about food, clothing, and shelter, the insane people in the area also have doctors to examine them and provide them with therapeutic medications. According to the report from the local management authority, in 1930, 53 leprosy patients escaped from the area privately, 125 died, 4 were cured and released, and 16 were transferred elsewhere. A total of 1,058 people were admitted and treated this year, of which 211 were newcomers. As of December 31, 1930, the registered number of leprosy patients was 860.

Within the area, there are 54 thatched cottages, each housing two or three people, totaling 143 insane people. In front of each cottage, there is a small lawn for the insane people to stroll. Those patients who are able to work are encouraged to grow vegetables and fruits. Therefore, during this year, most of the thatched cottages were planted with vegetables and fruits in the back.

In the return settlement, there are 14 shelters, each accommodating more than 20 people, totaling 384 patients. Most of the leprosy patients in these shelters have reached the first stage and are mostly disabled. In addition, there is a mixed-race leprosy shelter, accommodating 16 people, including two overseas Chinese students and one from the Philippines. As for the new settlement, there are currently seven shelters, housing 315 patients, of which 211 are newcomers. In 1929, there were only 218 patients in the area. In 1930, the period with the largest number of patients was July 7, when there were 884 patients.

Doctors distinguish the severity of the disease of all leprosy patients and administer appropriate medications. Those with severe illnesses are given pills, while those with milder illnesses are given injections. A total of 5,871 injections were given throughout the year. In addition, four people were released because they were completely cured.

In this settlement, there is a recreational team. When it was first established, there were 14 people. The coach is a person with injuries. They are already able to perform various recreational activities. In the mixed-race leprosy ward, there is also a military band, instructed by Filipinos living in the ward. They are progressing rapidly and have their own musical instruments. A pig farm is established in the settlement, supplying nearby residents with about 1,000 pigs each year. Some leprosy patients are addicted to opium. The authorities have also allocated them a certain amount, but the government has now ordered the gradual reduction of the allocation. There are a total of 295 opium addicts, of which 87 need to smoke only once a day, 87 need to smoke twice a day, and the other 119 need to smoke three times a day. All opium smokers are housed in the old settlement.

As for the strong patients, the government gives them a job, or they grow vegetables and fruits themselves, and other operations such as pig farming. All the rewards obtained belong to them. Patients who are unable to work are given a monthly allowance of one yuan by the government for miscellaneous expenses. Therefore, this leprosarium has become a paradise outside the world.

The Mount Erskine leprosarium is exclusively for men. As for the leprosarium for women, it is located in Jelutong, with a total of 79 patients, of which 18 are newcomers. Four people were also released because they were completely cured. The condition of the remaining people has also improved considerably. In one year, ten people escaped privately, eight died, and four were transferred elsewhere. As of December 31, 1930, there were only 54 women in the ward.

Saving the pitiful disabled and insane people is the compassion and responsibility that we humans should have. May we have organizations like this leprosarium on Penang Island overseas for the unfortunate and insane people in China.
